< Text>
The service here was great! I forgot the server's name but he was very friendly and helpful. We ended up getting plenty of fries. The chili cheese fries and cheese fries were crispy and savory with the perfect amount of cheese in each. The bacon and cheese tator tots had plenty of crispy bacon and the tots were crispy. I'd definitely recommend the chili cheese fries and bacon cheddar tots. We also had the Smoke House burger. It has bacon, cheddar, and bbq sauce. You have the option of making it a single or double. I was a little disappointed with this one. The description reads: "Thick-cut Applewood smoked bacon, crispy sourdough onion rings, Wisconsin Cheddar cheese & our special recipe Smoke House BBQ Ranch." It only had one piece of bacon folded into a V (not very thick either) so it looks like two and only one onion ring. The soda there is good but if you add a flavor shot (0.69), that's $4 a soda. Would come again but for the fries.<//Text>

He prescribed me pills for the infection on my wisdom tooth and the pain and told me to come back some other day and get my teeth pulled out. I made an appointment for the following friday with the specialist, because I was told that he was really good and fast at extracting wisdom teeth.
***
Okay so today is day 2 (wisdom teeth are out) and I can honestly say I feel good. I mean obviously yes it hurts a bit and my mouth feels weird having four holes in it, obviously. But my face is rarely swollen and the bleeding is very minimal so I am not complaining.
So if anyone ever needs their wisdom teeth removed I highly recommend you guys this Western Dental and ask for the specialist Sergey Sirenko. He only goes every other friday there but trust me he is great! My procedure lasted about 35-40 minutes. It was quick, got 4 shots of anestisia, waited for it to take effect, then got 6 more shots of anestisia, and finally he just took all four teeth out and that took less than 10 minutes. And I did not feel a thing. I felt slight pressure for the bottom molars but nothing else. He gave me strong meds so I havent felt horrible pain. My swollen cheeks only lasted while the anestisia was still in effect and now my cheeks are almost to regular size and they only feel a bit sore.
I can honestly say the dentist there are very good at their jobs and they talk to you with a great manner and they show they cared, unlike other dentist.
So highly recommend this specific Western Dental!</text>

<rating>3<//rating><Gmap_id>0x808fb5df5e082253:0xb0e5b62315f1a615<//Gmap_id>< Text>
Decent place to eat if you don't want to wait.  We have been many times and will probably be back.  It's not spectacular, but not horrible (hence the 3 stars).  They do like to use "Chef Mic" (microwave) often, but other than that seems okay.  We have been for the Sunday brunch and were not really impressed.  They have a lot of food, but it's all pretty forgettable.  The omelette, pancake, waffle station where they will make options on demand was pretty good and definitely fresh compared to the rest of the food.  The pie table was pretty good and a good deal as a pie there is pretty expensive.  So...go get and omelette and some pie and be happy.  They are not that busy, so I'm not sure how much longer they will be in business there...however, they have been there for some time and have survived, so who knows.  We will continue to go there as long as they are there.<//Text>

<review>To be clear, this review is solely based on my experiences ordering and picking up pies for Thanksgiving and Christmas this year.  I ordered three MC pies a few days before Thanksgiving. I had to park over by Michael's!  I was highly impressed to be greeted by a host at the front door and directed where to go upon my arrival. Just for the pie pickups alone, it was very well staffed with clusters of employees finding the order, another retrieving your pies, and another responsible for check-out. <Rating>4< /Rating>< review>
To be clear, this review is solely based on my experiences ordering and picking up pies for Thanksgiving and Christmas this year.  I ordered three MC pies a few days before Thanksgiving.  I did not sit on hold for too long and the customer service was very professional and courteous.  When I arrived the day before Thanksgiving to pick them up, the parking lot was absolute chaos!  I had to park over by Michael's!  I was highly impressed to be greeted by a host at the front door and directed where to go upon my arrival.  The pickup routine was organized very well (prepaid pies go through one direction/entrance and unpaid, pre-orders through another).  Just for the pie pickups alone, it was very well staffed with clusters of employees finding the order, another retrieving your pies, and another responsible for check-out.  I actually added my Banana Cream to my order and it was no problem.  I was in and out of there in minutes, the customer service was friendly and warm, there is a board kept updated and within a central view to see what pies are available in stock if you want to add to your order.  Not to mention, all of the sides they had prepared and wrapped and priced as well!  Very smooth, very easy, in and out!  Christmas Eve was much less crowded.  I pre-ordered online which was very convenient and even if I had lost my confirmation email, they have their own copy when you check in.  I hope to find time to go in and enjoy a meal there one of these days!  Also, their pies are outstanding!  We've had pumpkin, lemon meringue, banana cream, and lemon dream...They are all fantastic!</review>
